<text>So much rave about these Korea originated hot dog place, I had to pay a visit and try them myself.  At first when I arrived there, I couldn't find the place as it was a tiny confined space in the corner of the plaza food court.  Luckily, the place wasn't busy, just few people waiting for their order and no one on the line, surprising! as I was anticipating a long line especially around dinner time.  The price I thought was reasonable, original starting at $ 1.99 for original hot dog all the way to $ 3.99 I believe for squid hot dog.   Didn't take long to get my order and I had a choice to either dip it for sugar coating and I preferred not to.  They also had different types of sauces to top it which plays very important role in the taste of these hot dogs.  Otherwise, these hot dogs are unique that the batter was made with 'sticky rice' where it's more chewy compared to dry bread batter.  And other unique thing is that some has cheese inside.
All-in-all , it's definitely worth the try but nothing to die for.< /text><user_id>108109693006874101582<//user_id><Rating>4</Rating><date>1569019164823< /date>< gmapID>

<date>1569394993824< /date><Rating>5< /Rating><Review>I've gotten 4 out of my 5 piercings here and when friends ask me about where to get a piercing this is always the place I recommend. There are a few good shops in the area but The Exotic Body still stands out from the rest thanks to level of experience & profesionalism the staff have.

The owner can come across as a bit no-nonsense at times which I think can be off-putting to some people, but from my perspective it's really a good thing. The staff are all positive people with a good sense of humor, they just have a preference for responsible nonsense. Which is what you want from someone who's about to stab a needle through part of your body.

It's clear that the owner, and all the staff, not only love what they do but take it seriously. They understand that the art forms they practice create a permanent change to their clients bodies & come with risks, and because they understand this they make sure that everything's done right.

The place is always clean, they have ideal sterilization practices, they teach you about aftercare, they advocate the use of safe jewlery materials & design, and they help their customers to make informed decisions and  get through the piercing process as easily & painlessly as possible.

It is a little more expensive than other shops in the area, but not by a lot. In my opinion it's worth it for the quality & sense of security you get by going to such a top notch place. I trust the staff here and have always had positive experiences with them.

I've had piercings done here by both Samantha & Mike. Sam did my tongue piercing and my helix piercing & Mike did both of my genital piercings. They both did a fantastic job and (obviously) made a repeat customer out of me. I'll be going back here when it's time for my next piercing, and I recommend that anyone else who's looking to get a piercing choose The Exotic Body as well.</Review>< Pics>

She offered to show us more jewelry in the back so we followed her to the back room where she had asked to check my tunnel size. So I had taken my tunnel out to give her so she could check. She rudely advised that they don't want you to touch your ears and touch their doors. If she would have politely told me prior that she would remove my tunnel with gloves on her hands I would not have removed it myself. After she had removed my plug she then told me to wash my hands in a rude tone as well. I apologized and washed my hands. Then after she had pulled a few plug options from the back to show me I had decided I wanted to wait a little longer to buy my next size. She at that point mumbled under her breathe "seriously...?" Confused I said "yes?" because I had told her I was just browsing in the main room. Then she stated that she pulled all these options out for me and was very rude just because I didn't want to buy something right that second. She gave my tunnel back to me in the baggy she was holding it in. She then went straight to helping my girlfriend look for a new septum ring. She had not offered to put my tunnel back in. After sitting for a second, waiting, I finally decided I'm going to put my tunnel in myself so I grabbed a glove from the box on the wall to use since they don't want you to touch your ears. She then rudely said "Oh. You want your plug back?" I didn't know they didn't want customers touching their ears. Again if they would have stated that I would have gladly let her put my tunnel in my ear. But when she did put my tunnel back in my ear she was very rough with my ear and seemed angry as she put it in my ear and surprisingly made my ear hurt. Which isn't something that happens when I take my plugs in and out of my ears when cleaning them.
Then she told me I could wait for my girlfriend out in the front.
My girlfriend had let me know that she was super nice to her throughout helping her. But thinks that she was extremely rude to me and that it was unwarranted.
I will never go back to The Exotic Body, nor will I recommend this shop to anyone ever again.
Try Chief Piercing located downtown. They're just as clean and have a great jewelry selection except the customer service is 100% better than here.</review>

After reviewing The Exotic Body online, I went in yesterday to have two piercings done. I'm so glad I chose this place, they're a very well-run shop and were very knowledgeable. First, I must say that I've visited this establish three times. Twice to buy jewelry and once for a piercing service. I didn't have so much of a problem with the jewelry nor the piercing.  The problem that I had was with the deceptive business practices of the gentleman that helped me who I think might've been the owner.. It was at this point that he then said that they had an ATM machine there. Well I wasn't going to go to the bank and get money and come back so I used the ATM machine thinking that I would get a cash discount on the price of the jewelry or the service. I didn't on any of them, it was still the same price whether I paid in cash or by credit card.

Technically, he was not lying to me because it was cheaper for him but not me in that he didn't have to pay credit card fees and probably made either all or a portion of the ATM fees.  Granted it was my fault to believe him and return the 2nd and 3rd  time, but I am a trusting person and because of the location, the length of time it's been in business, it seemed like a reputable establishment.

All I have to say is caveat emptor, buyer beware.</review>

<rating>5</rating><Review>Amazing cappuccinos - they caramelize a touch of sugar on top to make it especially delish!  I‚Äôve had several of the croissants & they are flakey & filling (if you get one of the sandwiches).< /Review><pictures>None</pictures>< Resp>

<Time>1550541647264<//Time><Gmap_id>0x80db1ba433f8ed57:0x931b3d254028293b< /Gmap_id>< review>
We had brunch on President's Day at L'Atelier Cafe and really enjoyed it. I found them on Yelp and they were very highly rated as well as reasonably priced. They are a true French cafe, since the decor is French ("decor" being a French word), the ambiance is French (did you catch that "ambiance" is also a French word?), the menu was written in French and English (did you notice that "menu" is originally a French word?), the food was French, and the owners spoke French among themselves and to some of the customers.  I felt like I was in a cafe in the French countryside.

We ordered a couple of vegetarian croissants, each filled with 3 scrambled eggs, spinach, Gruyere cheese (French) and tomatoes. They came with a very high quality side salad, lightly dressed with a vinaigrette (French word!). They were truly delicious. They had simplicity, depth of flavor and that authenticity you will not find at a non-French cafe.

This cafe servers breakfast and lunch. Some other menu options include, quiche (French word!), omelette (French word!), sandwiches, including Jambon de Paris (I had to look that one up--it's a French style ham!),
Chicken, and Prosciutto. They also have crepes and, of course, French toast. Whew! We made it!

In short, I highly recommend you pay a visit to this cafe, as it is truly an experience beyond the food.<//review>

5< /rating>

<review>Doesn't get any better than this place. Been coming here for the past year or two with friends and they're always consistent. I'd say this place is on-par if not better than Howlin' Ray's, at least with the wait time that is.

<Text>Absolutely love it. We've been looking for a great French option, & now we found it, without having to fly to France

Well, we are back. No reason to visit Palm Springs without grabbing an amazing bite here.

They import their butter and flour from France and it shows. The Croissant is so DAM flakey it will be messy but worth any amount of mess. Stunning

Today got the French toast with bacon (with fruit) & Parrie Omlet.
Owned by couple from France and she takes your order, she's losing her accent (compared to last year).
With the croissant you get butter (yummy butter) & jelly, make sure you try it all 4 ways (Plain, butter, jelly, butter & jelly) before you judge the right way.

Essentially you can tell, we absolutely love this place, sit outside and enjoy the shade & breeze with the best French food outside of France.

We added an irde if fries with blue cheese, exquisite. Just enough blue cheese to add flavor without drowning them in cheese.

Every single person I have ever brought here insists on coming back, 3,4,5, ...10 times during their stay. Had the Veggie Croissant and it was perfect!!!The French lady (owner?) told me they make the croissant themselves in the shop. Great job! Warm, crunchy outside, soft buttery taste inside. Stuffed with 1 scrambled egg, cheese, spinach, avocado and tomato. A perfect start into the day.
Double shot Americano came in a porcelain cup with just the right  will of water to maintain an intense espresso taste.
I'll be back here again. The sooner the better ...</Review>

My wife and I have been to Palm Springs the past couple of years and "discovered" L'Atelier and make a point to always stop by for lunch. A food review:

Chocolate croissant was light and buttery with just enough chocolate to sweeten each bite.

Croque monsieur is a traditional French ham and cheese sandwich. Sturdy but soft pieces of bread cover simple pieces of unsalted ham adorned with melted cheese and white sauce. At this place, the gruyere cheese and bechamel sauce might tempt you back for more.

Was told that the bread is made in house except for the macarons.

Food came quickly-- service is friendly and leisurely.< /review>

<review>Very cute, cozy French bistro by authentic French owners. It is centrally, and at the same time, beautifully located at the walkable plaza in the heart of Palm Springs. I had the Petite Quiche Provencale that stands out with its goat cheese and combination of fine herbs. It was delicious. I added the L‚Äôatelier French pastries a mix of small pastries of butter croissant, chocolate croissant, and raisin roll. Great price $1.90, but know that they are really small if you have a bigger appetite for something sweet get a regular pastry. On the other hand, great for tasting from everything. The pastries are fluffy and buttery with its authentic croissant crisp. And of course, I had a caf√© latte which tasted smooth like European coffee. The couple that runs the caf√© is French and very nice. The only downfall is that it is so popular, but small, that it can be crowded and you have to wait in line for a while especially on the weekend.</review>< user_id>

Very cute, cozy French bistro by authentic French owners. It is centrally, and at the same time, beautifully located at the walkable plaza in the heart of Palm Springs. I had the Petite Quiche Provencale that stands out with its goat cheese and combination of fine herbs. It was delicious. I added the L‚Äôatelier French pastries a mix of small pastries of butter croissant, chocolate croissant, and raisin roll. Great price $1.90, but know that they are really small if you have a bigger appetite for something sweet get a regular pastry. On the other hand, great for tasting from everything. The pastries are fluffy and buttery with its authentic croissant crisp. And of course, I had a caf√© latte which tasted smooth like European coffee. The couple that runs the caf√© is French and very nice. The only downfall is that it is so popular, but small, that it can be crowded and you have to wait in line for a while especially on the weekend.<//Text>

< review>
We've been so lucky to find this little cafe. We have been welcomed by the owners, a young french couple who came to palm springs to bring a little piece of paris in the desert. We tried different dishes and everything was delicious, tasty and well presented.
We shared the cheese platter and it was amazing. Charlotte explained us how to eat it, from the mildest to the strongest and which cheese were on the platter and their origines. I really recommend the Saucisson sandwich with a side of soup (i had the carrot, goat cheese and coconut soup...very creative and so delicious). My husband tried the Smocked Duck salad and he loved it. He also tried a side of their house made fries. They serve the fries with a HM aioli which was also amazing. To finish with, we got an amazing latte and shared the raspberry tart which was scrumptious. All in all, we really recommend this place which serves excellent quality of food in a very cute decor with an amazing service. Thank you Charlotte & Raphael<//review>
